<H1><h><key1>RI</key1><key2>RI</key2></h><body>.<s>RI</s>¦ (<s>Ya</s>) <s>RIY</s> r. 1st cl. (<s>nayati-te</s>)<br/>²1 To conduct, to drive or guide, to cause progressive conveyance.<br/>²2 To obtain, to get. The root is inflected as the deponent verb, implying.<br/>²1 <i>Instruction,</i> as <s>nayate SAstre</s> he instructs in the <i>Sa4stra;</i><br/>²2 <i>Worshipping,</i> <s>vizRuMnayate</s> he worships VISHN'U; also with prepositions in the sense of;<br/>²1 <i>Paying,</i> <s>Bftyamupanayate</s> he pays the hire;<br/>²2 <i>Paying as a debt,</i> <s>fRamvinayate</s> he discharges the debt;<br/>²3 <i>Casting or lifting up,</i> <s>daRqamunnayate</s> he lifts up the stick;<br/>²4 <i>Giving,</i> <s>dravyambinayate</s> he gives the things; and<br/>²5 <i>Brahmanical Investiture,</i> <s>puttramupanayate</s> he invests his son with the thread: it is also deponent, governing an incorporeal object existing in the agent, as <s>kroDamvinayate</s> he suppresses wrath; if the object is not in the agent the verb is active, as <s>guroHktoDamvinayati</s> he appeases his teacher's anger; as also if the object is corporal, as <s>gaRqaM vinayati</s> he turns away the cheek. The root occurs with many prefixes, and in a great variety of meanings;<br/>²1 With <s>anu,</s> ^a To ask, to entreat. ^b To make like or resembling.<br/>²c To favour.<br/>²2 With <s>ap,</s> ^a To take away, to remove. ^b To attract.<br/>²3 With <s>aBi,</s><br/>²3 To indicate by signs. ^b To be kind or civil to.<br/>²4 With <s>AN,</s> To bring.<br/>²5 With <s>ut,</s> To raise up.<br/>²6 With <s>upa,</s> To approach, to go near to, (see also above.)<br/>²7 With <s>dur,</s> To act or behave wickedly.<br/>²8 With <s>nir,</s> ^a To get or obtain. ^b To ascertain, to determine.<br/>²9 With <s>pari,</s> ^a To marry. ^b To take cognizance of.<br/>²10 With <s>pra,</s><br/>²a To punish. ^b To love.<br/>²11 With <s>vi,</s> ^a To take away, to make remote or distant. ^b To be humble or modest.<br/>²12 With <s>vi</s> and <s>apa,</s> To remove, to dispel, to disperse.<br/>²13 With <s>vi</s> and <s>nir,</s> To decide by law.<br/>²14 With <s>sam,</s> ^a To collect. ^b To discharge.<br/>²15 With <s>san</s> and <s>anu,</s> To intreat.<br/>²16 With <s>sama</s> and <s>AN,</s> To assemble, to collect, &amp;c.</body><tail><L>16835</L><pc>361</pc></tail></H1>
